# CSC337: Coursework 1

## Task 1: Design 1
### Map showing the link between the authors, which are the primary creator(s) followed by all contributors,
### and the creators, the core creators of the resource.  

<b>Aim:</b> To find similarities and patterns between the creators and the authors in the dataset.

<b>Visual Design Type:</b> Text over a heatmap.

<b>Name of Tool:</b> Altair.

<b>Visual Mappings:</b>
+ The boxes with numbers in them are the interceptions of the data from the x and y axes.
+ The x-axis is represented by the authors' column.
+ The y-axis is represented by the creators' column.
+ The colors are easy to see, the chart easy to understand, but the shape of the boxes could be bigger.

<b>Data Preparation:</b> 
+ Used the head function to limit the data, since the result gets too big to read and takes a lot of computational power. 
+ Chose just the essential columns needed from the dataset.

<b>Improvements:</b> 
+ The main limitation is the space and computation power which stopped me from using the full dataset.
+ Another possible improvement would be to cross this design with another characteristic of the dataset and find new links, patterns and interesting information.
+ Animations can be added to make it interactive and better for viewing, in general.


<b>Image:</b> Can be found in its designated folder, in PNG format. 


```python
import pandas as pd
import geopandas as gpd
import altair as alt
import json
from vega_datasets import data
```


```python
# use the GPS coordinate reference system (WRS84 a.k.a EPSG:4326)
__coord_system__ = {'init': 'epsg:4326'}

# font to use for chart labels
__CHART_FONT__ = 'Circular'
```


```python
# load GPPD data set into pandas array
source = pd.read_csv('../data/pleiades-locations.csv').head(1000)

# keep a necessary columns
d_choro_geo = source[['geometry']]
```

```python
# Configure common options
base = alt.Chart(source).transform_aggregate(
    num_people='count()',
    groupby=['creators', 'authors']
).encode(
    alt.X('authors:O', scale=alt.Scale(paddingInner=0)),
    alt.Y('creators:O', scale=alt.Scale(paddingInner=0)),
)

# Configure heatmap
heatmap = base.mark_rect().encode(
    color=alt.Color('num_people:Q',
        scale=alt.Scale(scheme='viridis'),
        legend=alt.Legend(direction='horizontal')
    )
)

# Configure text
text = base.mark_text(baseline='middle').encode(
    text='num_people:Q',
    color=alt.condition(
        alt.datum.num_people > 100,
        alt.value('black'),
        alt.value('white')
    )
)

# Draw the chart
heatmap + text
```

    function loadScript(lib) {
      return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
        var s = document.createElement('script');
        s.src = paths[lib];
        s.async = true;
        s.onload = () => resolve(paths[lib]);
        s.onerror = () => reject(`Error loading script: ${paths[lib]}`);
        document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(s);
      });
    }

    function showError(err) {
      outputDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="error" style="color:red;">${err}</div>`;
      throw err;
    }

    function displayChart(vegaEmbed) {
      vegaEmbed(outputDiv, spec, embedOpt)
        .catch(err => showError(`Javascript Error: ${err.message}<br>This usually means there's a typo in your chart specification. See the javascript console for the full traceback.`));

      requirejs.config({paths});

      displayChart(vegaEmbed);

      loadScript("vega")
        .then(() => loadScript("vega-lite"))
        .then(() => loadScript("vega-embed"))
        .catch(showError)
        .then(() => displayChart(vegaEmbed));
